<Rate>2< /Rate><Review>This Plaza has a CVS 24 hour drug store. A clothing store for men, women and kids at good prices. It's not the Miller's Outpost it used to be, but it has affordable prices. The sub machine is one of the best in the entire Antelope Valley. The Asian restaurant I have had food poisoning from. Of course the Asian restaurant has changed hands numerous times. The monster Donuts has the most outrageous prices of any donut store in Southern California.
